Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, place it on a table, and press it as we said in gout, and let the patient lie on their healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit; et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And when the dislocation is forward, it is necessary to extend the affected leg quickly, as I have said; and the attendant must put effort on the affected leg, then press with the other hand, and extend it down towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches; et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table; et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz; adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve; et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus; et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors; puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And if the dislocation is outward, it is not necessary to extend the patient down or lift them from the ground, but it must be as if the hip were dislocated outward, as we said about lying on both hips; and let them be on their side, and the bandage extended as we said before, and one should press on the joint to the table; and it will be in place when the patient extends their legs and they are equal; then close the thighs, and apply the plaster, and tie it with a bandage, so that the hip does not move; and let them rest for three or four days, then loosen it and apply the plaster again; and if you see that they are equal, tie it as before, and leave it for three days; then loosen it, and allow the limb to move gently, until the limb is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The knee is dislocated in three ways: namely, inward, outward, and backward; and it does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez; et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez; puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement; et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And the signs are that you instruct the patient to bend their leg at the thigh, and if it does not fit at the thigh, know that it is dislocated; and the restoration for all of them is that you make the patient sit upright, and extend their leg if they can, and place your back against their side, and put their foot on your feet; then take their knee in your palms, and pull it between your fingers, then bend the two sides of the knee firmly; and another attendant extends their foot, so that the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that the leg fits well at the thigh slightly; and apply the plaster, and make the leg fit at the thigh, and tie them together tightly for three or four days, then loosen it; and the patient should not try to walk until the limb is strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not in place, administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	Of the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heel is sometimes displaced, and sometimes dislocated completely, inward and outward.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	And the sign is that the ankle is swollen, and protruding towards the part where it is dislocated: the repositioning is gentle, and it should be extended gently by hand when it is only displaced.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is completely dislocated, you must have the patient sit upright, and hold the leg above the ankle; then pull the foot towards your right hand, and then to the left twice, then extend it upwards, and push the foot upwards; and do this twice, as we have said, pushing and pulling the foot; if it returns, it is good; if not, repeat the procedure, because it returns; and if it cannot return thus, have the patient lie on their back on the ground, and place a firm stick in the ground between their thighs, and tie cloths around it, so it doesn't hurt the patient; then have an assistant hold the thigh, and another assistant extend the foot with their hands or with a rope, which they tie to the top of the foot; then each assistant extends equally, and the stick remains between the patient's thighs to restrain them when extending; then let the assistants align the dislocation with their hands, and another assistant hold the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it is in place, apply plaster and bandages, and bind it tightly, and tie the foot to the leg, and protect the nerves above the ankle behind, so the bandage is not too tight; then leave it for two or three days, and if the bandage softens, tighten it; then untie it on the third or fourth day, and forbid the patient from walking for four days; and if he walks before that time, there is no certainty that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if a painful abscess arises, you must treat it as we have described elsewhere, until it is healed.
des dois	of the fingers
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the fingers are dislocated, they should be gently extended without effort, and this is an easy task.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in any part of the back of the foot, you should have the patient sit on a flat surface or, i.e., a table, sitting straight, and place your foot over the exposed joints, then press firmly on your foot until it returns to its place; and when it is straight, and nothing is visible, place a table with two supports under the sole of the foot, then bind it firmly and leave it for three days, then untie it; and have him rest, until it is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound comes with a dislocation, and one wishes to restore it, many times the patient dies: therefore, do not be presumptuous in the treatment unless you are skilled in the art and have practiced it for a long time, and if you are compassionate and merciful and cautious, and not rash; and at the beginning, use soothing things for the hot abscess, and leave the patient in God's hand if you do not see hope for health; and when you see hope, then immediately return the limb to its place before the hot abscess arrives; and when the limb is in place, administer soothing things for the hot abscess, and treat the wound as necessary with drying ointments; and if with the dislocation there is a fracture and small bones separated, remove them, and do what we have said in simple illnesses; and beware of entering the path of fear, as I have said, for this will be to your disadvantage according to your Creator, and for the preservation of your spirit and body.
Amen	Amen.
